Gerald,

thanks for the update and implementing the suggested features.

My current project to re-create print versions of country profiles based on 
the factbool data makes steady progress. The infrastructure is in place and 
very functional. As you can see in the sample attached, the profiles 
contain the original flag, locator and map graphics. The version containing 
the 267 entities listed in the WFB compile to a 2300+ page document 
(without appendices etc) ...

The macros to render all the stuff are still brutally raw, but the result 
is not too bad.

Updating all profiles would require to run 3 scripts:

   1. download & convert all entries to JSON using your new version of the 
   factbook gem
   2. convert all JSON files to .tex macro calls and create custom main tex 
   files from template for all entries
   3. run latex in a for loop for all generated tex files
   4. as an option, run latex for the whole collection (the works)
   
I am thinking to setup a repo for the project. However, the Factbook in 
JSON is already online. What about joining forces?

Cheers
